Query Request Handler (HTTP Layer)\\n\\n**`pkg/api/ds_query.go`** — Entry point for the legacy `/ds/query` HTTP API. `QueryMetricsV2` receives the HTTP POST request, binds it to a `dtos.MetricRequest`, then calls `queryDataService.QueryData` or `QueryDataNew` depending on the `X-Query-V2` header. The response is serialized via `toJsonStreamingResponse`. The function `getDSQueryEndpoint` conditionally rewrites requests to the new Kubernetes API-server path (`/apis/query.grafana.app/v0alpha1/...`) when the `FlagQueryServiceRewrite` feature toggle is enabled.\\n\\n## 2. New Query API Server Handler\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`** — The Kubernetes API server-style query endpoint used by the new query service. `queryREST.Connect` handles incoming POST requests, parsing the body into `query.QueryDataRequest` and delegating to `handleQuery`. `handleQuery` marshals queries into `dtos.MetricRequest` format and calls `service.QueryData`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/register.go`** — Registers `QueryAPIBuilder`, wires up `newQueryREST`, `pluginsStorage`, expression query schemas, and the `singleTenantInstanceProvider` via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider`.\\n\\n## 3. Core Query Service — Dispatch Logic\\n\\n**`pkg/services/query/query.go`** — The central orchestration layer. `ServiceImpl.queryData` parses the metric request (`parseMetricRequest`), then:\\n- If expressions are present, delegates to `handleExpressions` → `expr.Service.TransformData`\\n- If targeting a single datasource, calls `handleQuerySingleDatasource` → `pluginClient.QueryData` (single-tenant) or `qsDsClient.QueryData` (query-service/multi-tenant)\\n- If multiple datasources, fans out via `executeConcurrentQueries`\\n\\nThe standalone `QueryData` function at the package level creates a `ServiceImpl` directly (used from the new API server path).\\n\\n## 4. Plugin Backend Query Dispatch\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`** — Defines the top-level `plugins.Client` interface (`type Client interface { backend.Handler }`) implemented by the plugin client stack.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/plugins.go`** — Defines `PluginClient` interface (combining `backend.QueryDataHandler`, `backend.CheckHealthHandler`, `backend.CallResourceHandler`, `backend.StreamHandler`, etc.) and the `Plugin.QueryData` forwarding method that calls through to the registered backend plugin.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`** — Concrete `Service` implementing `plugins.Client`. `QueryData` looks up the plugin in the registry by ID, dispatches `p.QueryData(ctx, req)` (which calls the plugin via gRPC), normalizes response frame RefIDs, and wraps errors with typed plugin error types.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/plugin.go`** — `pluginClient` implementing `clientapi.QueryDataClient`. `QueryData` checks access control (`CanQueryDataSource`), resolves `DataSourceInstanceSettings` via `plugincontext.Provider.GetDataSourceInstanceSettings`, builds a `backend.PluginContext` via `PluginContextForDataSource`, and dispatches to the underlying `plugins.Client.QueryData`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/instance_provider.go`** — `singleTenantInstanceProvider` / `singleTenantInstance`: wraps a `QueryDataClient` for the single-tenant flow; instantiated via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider` which takes the raw `plugins.Client`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/clientapi/clientapi.go`** — Defines the `QueryDataClient` interface, `Instance` interface, and `InstanceProvider` interface used throughout the query-service path.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dsquerierclient/qs_datasource_client_builder.go`** — `QSDatasourceClientBuilder` interface and implementations that bridge the legacy `ServiceImpl` to the new query-service client (multi-tenant or null/no-op for single-tenant). `QsDatasourceClientBuilderWithInstance` delegates to the `Instance.GetDataSourceClient`.\\n\\n**`pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go`** — `PluginHandler.QueryDataHandler()`: the aggregator-side HTTP handler for plugin QueryData requests (used in the plugin aggregation API server), which dispatches directly to `h.client.QueryData` and wraps the result as `aggregationv0alpha1.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/querier.go`** — `DefaultQuerier` wraps a `plugins.Client` to implement the `Querier` interface used in the per-datasource API server flows.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`** — Registers datasource API groups and defines the `PluginClient` interface subset (QueryData, CheckHealth, CallResource, ConversionHandler) used by datasource API servers.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/queryconvert.go`** — `queryConvertREST` handles the query-convert subresource, parsing incoming HTTP requests into `query.QueryDataRequest` format.\\n\\n## 5. Plugin Context Resolution\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go`** — `Provider.GetWithDataSource` and `Provider.PluginContextForDataSource` resolve `backend.PluginContext` (including `DataSourceInstanceSettings`) from the datasource model and plugin store before dispatching queries.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/adapters/adapters.go`** — `ModelToInstanceSettings` converts a `datasources.DataSource` database model to `backend.DataSourceInstanceSettings`, decrypting secure JSON data.\\n\\n## 6. Query Response Transformation\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/transform.go`** — `Service.TransformData` runs server-side expression evaluation over datasource query results, executing math, reduce, threshold, SQL, and other expression node types to produce the final `backend.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/service.go`** — Defines `expr.Service` (the expression service with `TransformData`) and the `ResultConverter` field used to convert datasource frame results for expression pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/converter.go`** — `ResultConverter.Convert` transforms raw `data.Frames` from datasource query responses into formats suitable for use in expression node pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/query_convert.go`** — `ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest` bridges the `backend.QueryDataRequest` format to the k8s-style `data.QueryDataRequest` used in the multi-tenant query-service flow (called from `handleQuerySingleDatasource`).\\n\\n## 7. Middleware Stack\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`** — `CachingMiddleware.QueryData` wraps the plugin client call with query result caching (via `CachingService.HandleQueryRequest`). The same directory contains other middleware that adds OAuth tokens, user headers, tracing, metrics, and request deduplication to every plugin query.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/caching/service.go`** — Defines the `CachingService` interface with `HandleQueryRequest` (check cache before querying) and `CachedQueryDataResponse` (with an `UpdateCacheFn` to store results after querying).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":97935,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"207d9877-3d6f-4184-89ba-7a85422b0546","uuid":"b28b1080-d3b6-412f-b6d3-1d4780f65682"}

The function `getDSQueryEndpoint` conditionally rewrites requests to the new Kubernetes API-server path (`/apis/query.grafana.app/v0alpha1/...`) when the `FlagQueryServiceRewrite` feature toggle is enabled.\\n\\n## 2. New Query API Server Handler\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`** — The Kubernetes API server-style query endpoint used by the new query service. `queryREST.Connect` handles incoming POST requests, parsing the body into `query.QueryDataRequest` and delegating to `handleQuery`. `handleQuery` marshals queries into `dtos.MetricRequest` format and calls `service.QueryData`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/register.go`** — Registers `QueryAPIBuilder`, wires up `newQueryREST`, `pluginsStorage`, expression query schemas, and the `singleTenantInstanceProvider` via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider`.\\n\\n## 3. Core Query Service — Dispatch Logic\\n\\n**`pkg/services/query/query.go`** — The central orchestration layer. `ServiceImpl.queryData` parses the metric request (`parseMetricRequest`), then:\\n- If expressions are present, delegates to `handleExpressions` → `expr.Service.TransformData`\\n- If targeting a single datasource, calls `handleQuerySingleDatasource` → `pluginClient.QueryData` (single-tenant) or `qsDsClient.QueryData` (query-service/multi-tenant)\\n- If multiple datasources, fans out via `executeConcurrentQueries`\\n\\nThe standalone `QueryData` function at the package level creates a `ServiceImpl` directly (used from the new API server path).\\n\\n## 4. Plugin Backend Query Dispatch\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`** — Defines the top-level `plugins.Client` interface (`type Client interface { backend.Handler }`) implemented by the plugin client stack.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/plugins.go`** — Defines `PluginClient` interface (combining `backend.QueryDataHandler`, `backend.CheckHealthHandler`, `backend.CallResourceHandler`, `backend.StreamHandler`, etc.) and the `Plugin.QueryData` forwarding method that calls through to the registered backend plugin.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`** — Concrete `Service` implementing `plugins.Client`. `QueryData` looks up the plugin in the registry by ID, dispatches `p.QueryData(ctx, req)` (which calls the plugin via gRPC), normalizes response frame RefIDs, and wraps errors with typed plugin error types.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/plugin.go`** — `pluginClient` implementing `clientapi.QueryDataClient`. `QueryData` checks access control (`CanQueryDataSource`), resolves `DataSourceInstanceSettings` via `plugincontext.Provider.GetDataSourceInstanceSettings`, builds a `backend.PluginContext` via `PluginContextForDataSource`, and dispatches to the underlying `plugins.Client.QueryData`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/instance_provider.go`** — `singleTenantInstanceProvider` / `singleTenantInstance`: wraps a `QueryDataClient` for the single-tenant flow; instantiated via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider` which takes the raw `plugins.Client`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/clientapi/clientapi.go`** — Defines the `QueryDataClient` interface, `Instance` interface, and `InstanceProvider` interface used throughout the query-service path.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dsquerierclient/qs_datasource_client_builder.go`** — `QSDatasourceClientBuilder` interface and implementations that bridge the legacy `ServiceImpl` to the new query-service client (multi-tenant or null/no-op for single-tenant). `QsDatasourceClientBuilderWithInstance` delegates to the `Instance.GetDataSourceClient`.\\n\\n**`pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go`** — `PluginHandler.QueryDataHandler()`: the aggregator-side HTTP handler for plugin QueryData requests (used in the plugin aggregation API server), which dispatches directly to `h.client.QueryData` and wraps the result as `aggregationv0alpha1.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/querier.go`** — `DefaultQuerier` wraps a `plugins.Client` to implement the `Querier` interface used in the per-datasource API server flows.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`** — Registers datasource API groups and defines the `PluginClient` interface subset (QueryData, CheckHealth, CallResource, ConversionHandler) used by datasource API servers.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/queryconvert.go`** — `queryConvertREST` handles the query-convert subresource, parsing incoming HTTP requests into `query.QueryDataRequest` format.\\n\\n## 5. Plugin Context Resolution\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go`** — `Provider.GetWithDataSource` and `Provider.PluginContextForDataSource` resolve `backend.PluginContext` (including `DataSourceInstanceSettings`) from the datasource model and plugin store before dispatching queries.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/adapters/adapters.go`** — `ModelToInstanceSettings` converts a `datasources.DataSource` database model to `backend.DataSourceInstanceSettings`, decrypting secure JSON data.\\n\\n## 6. Query Response Transformation\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/transform.go`** — `Service.TransformData` runs server-side expression evaluation over datasource query results, executing math, reduce, threshold, SQL, and other expression node types to produce the final `backend.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/service.go`** — Defines `expr.Service` (the expression service with `TransformData`) and the `ResultConverter` field used to convert datasource frame results for expression pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/converter.go`** — `ResultConverter.Convert` transforms raw `data.Frames` from datasource query responses into formats suitable for use in expression node pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/query_convert.go`** — `ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest` bridges the `backend.QueryDataRequest` format to the k8s-style `data.QueryDataRequest` used in the multi-tenant query-service flow (called from `handleQuerySingleDatasource`).\\n\\n## 7. Middleware Stack\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`** — `CachingMiddleware.QueryData` wraps the plugin client call with query result caching (via `CachingService.HandleQueryRequest`). The same directory contains other middleware that adds OAuth tokens, user headers, tracing, metrics, and request deduplication to every plugin query.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/caching/service.go`** — Defines the `CachingService` interface with `HandleQueryRequest` (check cache before querying) and `CachedQueryDataResponse` (with an `UpdateCacheFn` to store results after querying).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
